/-! ### Disjoint Variable Properties -/

/-
ARCHIVED (Phase 5): DV theorems with syntax errors (inl/inr ‚Üí intro/tail pattern change).
Will be rewritten in Phase 8 if needed.

/-- DV relation is symmetric -/
theorem dv_symmetric (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (v w : Variable) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars [(v, w)] œÉ ‚Üí Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars [(w, v)] œÉ := by
  intro h
  unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK at *
  intro v' w' hvw
  simp at hvw
  cases hvw with
  | inl heq =>
    have ‚ü®hv, hw‚ü© := heq
    subst hv hw
    have := h w v (by simp)
    intro x hx
    have := h w v (by simp)
    intro hxw
    exact this hxw hx
  | inr contra => simp at contra

/-- DV relation is not reflexive when substitution has variables -/
theorem dv_not_reflexive (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (v : Variable) :
  Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars (œÉ v) ‚â† [] ‚Üí
  ¬¨ Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars [(v, v)] œÉ := by
  intro hne
  unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK
  intro h
  -- Apply h to (v,v) which is in the list
  have hvv := h v v (by simp)
  -- varsInExpr vars (œÉ v) is non-empty by assumption
  -- But hvv says: ‚àÄ x ‚àà varsInExpr vars (œÉ v), x ‚àâ varsInExpr vars (œÉ v)
  -- This is contradiction: take any x in the list
  unfold Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr at *
  cases h_list : (œÉ v).syms.filterMap (fun s => let v := Variable.mk s; if v ‚àà vars then some v else none) with
  | nil => contradiction  -- hne says list is non-empty
  | cons x xs =>
    -- x is in the list
    have hx : x ‚àà x :: xs := List.mem_cons_self
    -- But hvv says x ‚àâ (x :: xs)
    rw [h_list] at hvv
    have : x ‚àâ x :: xs := hvv x hx
    contradiction
-/

/-- Weakening: More DV constraints ‚Üí harder to satisfy (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem dv_weakening (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  dv‚ÇÅ ‚äÜ dv‚ÇÇ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÇ œÉ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÅ œÉ := by
  intro hsub hok
  unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK at *
  intro v w hvw
  exact hok v w (hsub hvw)

/-- Appending DV lists preserves okness (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem dv_append (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÅ œÉ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÇ œÉ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars (dv‚ÇÅ ++ dv‚ÇÇ) œÉ := by
  intro h1 h2
  unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK at *
  intro v w hvw
  simp [List.mem_append] at hvw
  match hvw with
  | Or.inl hl => exact h1 v w hl
  | Or.inr hr => exact h2 v w hr

/-- Single DV pair check (needs proof update for new varsInExpr) -/
theorem dv_single_ok (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (v w : Variable) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars [(v, w)] œÉ ‚Üî
  (‚àÄ x, x ‚àà Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars (œÉ v) ‚Üí x ‚àâ Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars (œÉ w)) := by
  constructor
  ¬∑ intro h
    exact h v w (by simp)
  ¬∑ intro h
    unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK
    intro v' w' hvw
    simp at hvw
    have ‚ü®hv, hw‚ü© := hvw
    subst hv hw
    exact h

/-- DV constraints are independent (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem dv_independent (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst)
    (v w : Variable)
    (hdv : Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv œÉ)
    (hnotin : (v, w) ‚àâ dv) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars ((v, w) :: dv) œÉ ‚Üî
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars [(v, w)] œÉ ‚àß Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv œÉ := by
  constructor
  ¬∑ intro h
    constructor
    ¬∑ exact dv_weakening vars [(v,w)] ((v,w)::dv) œÉ (by simp) h
    ¬∑ exact dv_weakening vars dv ((v,w)::dv) œÉ (fun x hx => by simp [hx]) h
  ¬∑ intro ‚ü®h1, h2‚ü©
    exact dv_append vars [(v,w)] dv œÉ h1 h2

/-! ### DV Library (Algebra for Disjoint Variables)

Following GPT-5's recommendation: make DV reasoning algebraic with composition
and monotonicity lemmas.
-/

/-- DV is monotonic under subset refinement of constraints -/
theorem dvOK_mono (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  dv‚ÇÅ ‚äÜ dv‚ÇÇ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÇ œÉ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÅ œÉ := by
  -- This is just dv_weakening with different name for clarity
  exact dv_weakening vars dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ œÉ

/-- DV conjunction: dvOK on union iff dvOK on each part -/
theorem dvOK_conj (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars (dv‚ÇÅ ++ dv‚ÇÇ) œÉ ‚Üî
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÅ œÉ ‚àß Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv‚ÇÇ œÉ := by
  constructor
  ¬∑ intro h
    constructor
    ¬∑ exact dv_weakening vars dv‚ÇÅ (dv‚ÇÅ ++ dv‚ÇÇ) œÉ (fun x hx => by simp [hx]) h
    ¬∑ exact dv_weakening vars dv‚ÇÇ (dv‚ÇÅ ++ dv‚ÇÇ) œÉ (fun x hx => by simp [hx]) h
  ¬∑ intro ‚ü®h1, h2‚ü©
    exact dv_append vars dv‚ÇÅ dv‚ÇÇ œÉ h1 h2

/-- DV under substitution composition: if œÉ‚ÇÅ satisfies DV and œÉ‚ÇÇ preserves disjointness -/
theorem dvOK_subst_comp (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (dv : List (Variable √ó Variable)) (œÉ‚ÇÅ œÉ‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv œÉ‚ÇÅ ‚Üí
  (‚àÄ v w, (v, w) ‚àà dv ‚Üí
    ‚àÄ x, x ‚àà Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars (Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ v)) ‚Üí
         x ‚àâ Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars (Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ w))) ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK vars dv (fun v => Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ v)) := by
  intro h1 h2
  unfold Metamath.Spec.dvOK at *
  intro v w hvw
  exact h2 v w hvw

/-! ### Expression Properties -/

/-- Expression equality is decidable (structural) (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
instance expr_eq_dec (e‚ÇÅ e‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
  Decidable (e‚ÇÅ = e‚ÇÇ) := by
  -- DecidableEq derived automatically for Expr
  exact inferInstance

/-- Variables in expression are finite: list length bounded by symbol count (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem varsInExpr_finite (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (e : Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
  (Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars e).length ‚â§ e.syms.length := by
  -- filterMap produces at most as many elements as the input list
  unfold Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr
  apply List.length_filterMap_le

/-! ### Provability Properties -/

/-- Nil proof has empty stack (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem proofValid_nil_stack :
  ‚àÄ (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame) (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr),
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack [] ‚Üí
  stack = [] := by
  intro Œì fr stack hpv
  cases hpv
  rfl

/-- Proof validity inversion: nil case (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem proofValid_nil_iff (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame) (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack [] ‚Üî stack = [] := by
  constructor
  ¬∑ exact proofValid_nil_stack Œì fr stack
  ¬∑ intro h
    subst h
    exact Metamath.Spec.ProofValid.nil fr

/-- Steps list non-empty means stack non-empty (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
theorem proofValid_steps_nonempty_stack_nonempty :
  ‚àÄ (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (steps : List Metamath.Spec.ProofStep),
  steps ‚â† [] ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack steps ‚Üí
  stack ‚â† [] := by
  intro Œì fr stack steps hne hpv
  intro hempty
  subst hempty
  cases hpv
  ¬∑ simp at hne  -- nil case contradicts steps ‚â† []
  all_goals { simp }  -- All other constructors produce non-empty stack

/-- Frame equality is decidable (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
instance frame_eq_dec (fr‚ÇÅ fr‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Frame) :
  Decidable (fr‚ÇÅ = fr‚ÇÇ) := by
  exact inferInstance

/-- Hypothesis equality is decidable (PROVEN ‚úì) -/
instance hyp_eq_dec (h‚ÇÅ h‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Hyp) :
  Decidable (h‚ÇÅ = h‚ÇÇ) := by
  exact inferInstance

-- NOTE: Removed empty_proof_empty_conclusion - statement was incorrect.
-- Even with empty frame (fr.mand = []), we can prove complex expressions
-- via axioms (using useAxiom). The theorem would need significant revision
-- to be meaningful, and it's not used anywhere in the current proofs.

/-- Helper: ProofValid is monotone in Database -/
theorem proofValid_monotone (Œì‚ÇÅ Œì‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (steps : List Metamath.Spec.ProofStep) :
  (‚àÄ l fr' e', Œì‚ÇÅ l = some (fr', e') ‚Üí Œì‚ÇÇ l = some (fr', e')) ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì‚ÇÅ fr stack steps ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì‚ÇÇ fr stack steps := by
  sorry

/-- Provability is monotone: more axioms ‚Üí more provable -/
theorem provability_monotone (Œì‚ÇÅ Œì‚ÇÇ : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame) (e : Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
  (‚àÄ l fr' e', Œì‚ÇÅ l = some (fr', e') ‚Üí Œì‚ÇÇ l = some (fr', e')) ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.Provable Œì‚ÇÅ fr e ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.Provable Œì‚ÇÇ fr e := by
  intro h_subset ‚ü®steps, finalStack, hpv, h_final‚ü©
  exists steps, finalStack
  constructor
  ¬∑ exact proofValid_monotone Œì‚ÇÅ Œì‚ÇÇ fr finalStack steps h_subset hpv
  ¬∑ exact h_final

/-! ### Phase 2: Proof Validity Inversion Lemmas

Per GPT-5 guidance: These are critical for stepNormal_sound.
They let us treat the spec as cutpoints during the main proof.
-/

/-- Inversion for useEssential: extract essential hypothesis info -/
theorem proofValid_useEssential_inv (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (steps : List Metamath.Spec.ProofStep)
    (e : Metamath.Spec.Expr) (h_e : Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e) :
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack (Metamath.Spec.ProofStep.useHyp h_e :: steps) ‚Üí
  h_e ‚àà fr.mand ‚àß
  ‚àÉ prev_stack, stack = e :: prev_stack ‚àß
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr prev_stack steps := by
  intro hpv
  cases hpv with
  | useEssential fr' stack' steps' e' h_mem hpv' =>
    -- The constructor guarantees h_e = Hyp.essential e' and h_mem : h_e ‚àà fr.mand
    constructor
    ¬∑ exact h_mem
    ¬∑ exists stack'
      constructor
      ¬∑ rfl
      ¬∑ exact hpv'
  | _ => contradiction  -- Other constructors don't match

/-- Inversion for useFloating: extract floating hypothesis info -/
theorem proofValid_useFloating_inv (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (steps : List Metamath.Spec.ProofStep)
    (c : Metamath.Spec.Constant) (v : Metamath.Spec.Variable) :
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack (Metamath.Spec.ProofStep.useHyp (Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v) :: steps) ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v ‚àà fr.mand ‚àß
  ‚àÉ prev_stack, stack = ‚ü®c, [v.v]‚ü© :: prev_stack ‚àß
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr prev_stack steps := by
  intro hpv
  cases hpv with
  | useFloating stack' steps' c' v' h_mem hpv' =>
    constructor
    ¬∑ exact h_mem
    ¬∑ exists stack'
      constructor
      ¬∑ rfl
      ¬∑ exact hpv'
  | _ => contradiction

/-- Inversion for useAxiom: extract axiom application info (HARDEST) -/
theorem proofValid_useAxiom_inv (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (steps : List Metamath.Spec.ProofStep)
    (l : Metamath.Spec.Label) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack (Metamath.Spec.ProofStep.useAssertion l œÉ :: steps) ‚Üí
  ‚àÉ (fr' : Metamath.Spec.Frame) (e : Metamath.Spec.Expr) (prev_stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr),
    Œì l = some (fr', e) ‚àß
    Metamath.Spec.dvOK fr.vars fr.dv œÉ ‚àß
    Metamath.Spec.dvOK fr'.vars fr'.dv œÉ ‚àß
    Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr prev_stack steps ‚àß
    (let needed := fr'.mand.map (fun h => match h with
      | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e => Metamath.Spec.applySubst fr'.vars œÉ e
      | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v => œÉ v)
     prev_stack = needed.reverse ++ stack.tail ‚àß
     stack = Metamath.Spec.applySubst fr'.vars œÉ e :: stack.tail) := by
  intro hpv
  cases hpv with
  | useAxiom stack_prev steps_prev l_inner fr'' e' œÉ_inner h_db h_dv_fr h_dv_fr' hpv_prev needed_inner h_needed remaining h_remaining =>
    -- useAxiom gives us:
    -- - stack_prev = needed_inner.reverse ++ remaining (h_remaining)
    -- - conclusion stack = applySubst œÉ_inner e' :: remaining
    -- We need to show the conclusion stack equals our input stack
    exists fr'', e', stack_prev
    constructor; exact h_db
    constructor; exact h_dv_fr
    constructor; exact h_dv_fr'
    constructor; exact hpv_prev
    constructor
    ¬∑ -- prev_stack = needed.reverse ++ stack.tail
      -- stack = applySubst œÉ e' :: remaining (from useAxiom conclusion)
      -- stack.tail = remaining
      -- stack_prev = needed_inner.reverse ++ remaining (from h_remaining)
      -- So: stack_prev = needed_inner.reverse ++ stack.tail
      rw [h_remaining]
      congr 1
      -- Show that stack = applySubst œÉ e' :: remaining, so tail = remaining
      -- This is definitional from the useAxiom constructor's conclusion
      rfl
    ¬∑ -- stack = applySubst œÉ e' :: stack.tail
      -- The useAxiom constructor concludes with: applySubst œÉ e' :: remaining
      -- And we just showed stack.tail = remaining
      -- So: stack = applySubst œÉ e' :: stack.tail
      rfl
  | _ => contradiction

/-! ### Phase 3: Unification (Two-Phase Bind/Check)

Per GPT-5 guidance: Split unification into two phases to avoid substitution threading issues.

**Phase B1: matchFloats** - Bind variables from floating hypotheses only
**Phase B2: checkEssentials** - Check essential hypotheses match (no new bindings)

This design:
- Aligns with Metamath execution model (floats bind, essentials check)
- Avoids "œÉ‚ÇÇ extending œÉ‚ÇÅ" composition issues
- Uses algebra pack for DV reasoning
- Provides clear spec cutpoints for stepNormal_sound
-/

/-- Build substitution by matching symbols pairwise (helper for matchExpr).
    Returns a substitution œÉ such that applying it to hyp_syms gives stack_syms. -/
def matchSyms (tc : Metamath.Spec.Constant) (hyp_syms stack_syms : List Metamath.Spec.Sym) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
    Option Metamath.Spec.Subst :=
  match hyp_syms, stack_syms with
  | [], [] => some œÉ  -- Success: all matched
  | [], _ :: _ => none  -- Mismatch: stack has extra symbols
  | _ :: _, [] => none  -- Mismatch: hyp has extra symbols
  | h :: hs, s :: ss =>
      -- Check if h is a variable
      if h_var : h.length > 0 ‚àß h.get (‚ü®0, h_var.1‚ü© : Fin h.length) = 'v' then
        let v : Metamath.Spec.Variable := ‚ü®h‚ü©
        -- Check if v already has a binding
        match œÉ v with
        | ‚ü®_, [existing_sym]‚ü© =>
            -- v is bound: check consistency
            if existing_sym = s then
              matchSyms tc hs ss œÉ  -- Consistent, continue
            else
              none  -- Inconsistent: v maps to two different symbols
        | ‚ü®_, _‚ü© =>
            -- v is not yet bound to a single symbol, bind it now
            let œÉ' := fun w => if w = v then ‚ü®tc, [s]‚ü© else œÉ w
            matchSyms tc hs ss œÉ'
      else
        -- h is a constant: must match exactly
        if h = s then
          matchSyms tc hs ss œÉ
        else
          none
termination_by hyp_syms.length

/-- Attempt to match a hypothesis expression against a stack expression.
    Returns a substitution œÉ such that applySubst œÉ hyp = stackExpr.
    Only variables in hyp are bound (left-biased unification). -/
def matchExpr (hyp : Metamath.Spec.Expr) (stackExpr : Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
    Option Metamath.Spec.Subst :=
  -- Check typecodes match
  if hyp.typecode ‚â† stackExpr.typecode then none
  else
    -- Start with identity substitution
    let id_subst : Metamath.Spec.Subst := fun v => ‚ü®hyp.typecode, [v.v]‚ü©
    matchSyms hyp.typecode hyp.syms stackExpr.syms id_subst

/-- Helper: matchSyms only modifies variables that appear in hyp_syms -/
theorem matchSyms_preserves_domain (tc : Metamath.Spec.Constant) (hyp_syms stack_syms : List Metamath.Spec.Sym)
    (œÉ_init œÉ_result : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (v : Metamath.Spec.Variable) :
  matchSyms tc hyp_syms stack_syms œÉ_init = some œÉ_result ‚Üí
  v.v ‚àâ hyp_syms ‚Üí
  œÉ_result v = œÉ_init v := by
  intro h_match h_not_in
  induction hyp_syms, stack_syms using matchSyms.induct tc œÉ_init with
  | case1 => simp [matchSyms] at h_match; rw [h_match]
  | case2 => simp [matchSyms] at h_match
  | case3 => simp [matchSyms] at h_match
  | case4 h hs s ss ih =>
    simp at h_not_in
    unfold matchSyms at h_match
    split at h_match
    ¬∑ -- h is a variable
      next h_var =>
        split at h_match
        ¬∑ -- Already bound
          next existing h_existing =>
            split at h_match
            ¬∑ next h_eq => exact ih h_match h_not_in.2
            ¬∑ contradiction
        ¬∑ -- Bind it now
          next h_not_single =>
            have ih_applied := ih h_match h_not_in.2
            simp [ih_applied]
            split
            ¬∑ next h_v_eq =>
              -- v = ‚ü®h‚ü©, but h ‚àâ hs and v.v ‚àâ [h] ++ hs, contradiction
              have : v.v = h := by simp [Metamath.Spec.Variable.v] at h_v_eq; exact h_v_eq
              exact absurd this h_not_in.1
            ¬∑ rfl
    ¬∑ -- h is a constant
      next h_const =>
        split at h_match
        ¬∑ next h_eq => exact ih h_match h_not_in.2
        ¬∑ contradiction

/-- Soundness of matchSyms: if matching succeeds, applying the substitution gives the target -/
theorem matchSyms_sound (tc : Metamath.Spec.Constant) (hyp_syms stack_syms : List Metamath.Spec.Sym)
    (œÉ_init œÉ_result : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  matchSyms tc hyp_syms stack_syms œÉ_init = some œÉ_result ‚Üí
  hyp_syms.bind (fun s =>
    if h : s.length > 0 ‚àß s.get (‚ü®0, h.1‚ü© : Fin s.length) = 'v'
    then ((œÉ_result ‚ü®s‚ü© : Metamath.Spec.Expr)).syms
    else [s]) = stack_syms := by
  intro h_match
  -- Induction on hyp_syms
  induction hyp_syms, stack_syms using matchSyms.induct tc œÉ_init with
  | case1 =>
    -- hyp_syms = [], stack_syms = []
    simp [matchSyms] at h_match
    simp [List.bind]
  | case2 s ss =>
    -- hyp_syms = [], stack_syms = s :: ss
    simp [matchSyms] at h_match
  | case3 h hs =>
    -- hyp_syms = h :: hs, stack_syms = []
    simp [matchSyms] at h_match
  | case4 h hs s ss ih =>
    -- hyp_syms = h :: hs, stack_syms = s :: ss
    simp [List.bind]
    unfold matchSyms at h_match
    split at h_match
    ¬∑ -- h is a variable
      next h_var =>
        let v : Metamath.Spec.Variable := ‚ü®h‚ü©
        -- Split on whether v is already bound
        split at h_match
        ¬∑ -- v already bound to [existing_sym]
          next existing_sym h_existing =>
            split at h_match
            ¬∑ -- existing_sym = s, consistent
              next h_eq =>
                -- IH applies: matchSyms succeeded on tail
                have ih_applied := ih h_match
                -- matchSyms didn't change œÉ for v (v not in hs)
                have h_v_preserved : œÉ_result v = œÉ_init v := by
                  apply matchSyms_preserves_domain tc hs ss œÉ_init œÉ_result v h_match
                  intro h_contra
                  -- v.v = h, but h cannot be in hs (distinct symbols in pattern)
                  sorry  -- Need list distinctness or accept for now
                -- So œÉ_result v = œÉ_init v = ‚ü®_, [existing_sym]‚ü© = ‚ü®_, [s]‚ü©
                simp [h_var]
                rw [h_v_preserved, h_existing]
                simp [h_eq]
                exact ih_applied
            ¬∑ -- existing_sym ‚â† s, inconsistent ‚Üí none
              contradiction
        ¬∑ -- v not bound to single symbol, bind it now
          next h_not_single =>
            -- Updated œÉ' = fun w => if w = v then ‚ü®tc, [s]‚ü© else œÉ_init w
            -- IH applies with œÉ'
            have ih_applied := ih h_match
            -- v not in hs, so œÉ_result v = œÉ' v = ‚ü®tc, [s]‚ü©
            have h_v_preserved : œÉ_result v = (fun w => if w = v then ‚ü®tc, [s]‚ü© else œÉ_init w) v := by
              apply matchSyms_preserves_domain tc hs ss (fun w => if w = v then ‚ü®tc, [s]‚ü© else œÉ_init w) œÉ_result v h_match
              intro h_contra
              sorry  -- Same as above
            simp [h_var, h_v_preserved]
            exact ih_applied
    ¬∑ -- h is a constant
      next h_const =>
        split at h_match
        ¬∑ -- h = s
          next h_eq =>
            have ih_applied := ih h_match
            simp [h_const, h_eq]
            exact ih_applied
        ¬∑ -- h ‚â† s ‚Üí none
          contradiction

/-- Soundness of matchExpr: if matching succeeds, substitution is correct -/
theorem matchExpr_sound (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (hyp stackExpr : Metamath.Spec.Expr) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  matchExpr hyp stackExpr = some œÉ ‚Üí
  Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ hyp = stackExpr := by
  intro h_match
  unfold matchExpr at h_match
  split at h_match
  ¬∑ -- Typecode mismatch
    contradiction
  ¬∑ -- Typecodes match
    next h_tc_eq =>
      have h_syms := matchSyms_sound hyp.typecode hyp.syms stackExpr.syms
        (fun v => ‚ü®hyp.typecode, [v.v]‚ü©) œÉ h_match
      unfold Metamath.Spec.applySubst
      simp only []
      congr 1
      ¬∑ -- Typecodes equal (h_tc_eq : ¬¨(tc1 ‚â† tc2))
        simp only [show hyp.typecode = stackExpr.typecode by
          by_contra h
          exact h_tc_eq (Ne.symm h)]
      ¬∑ -- Symbols equal after substitution
        sorry  -- Need to adapt proof for vars parameter

/-- Domain of matchExpr: only affects variables in hyp -/
theorem matchExpr_domain (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (hyp stackExpr : Metamath.Spec.Expr) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  matchExpr hyp stackExpr = some œÉ ‚Üí
  ‚àÄ v : Metamath.Spec.Variable,
    v ‚àâ Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr vars hyp ‚Üí
    œÉ v = ‚ü®hyp.typecode, [v.v]‚ü© := by
  intro h_match v h_not_in
  unfold matchExpr at h_match
  split at h_match
  ¬∑ contradiction
  ¬∑ next h_tc_eq =>
      -- Apply preservation lemma
      apply matchSyms_preserves_domain hyp.typecode hyp.syms stackExpr.syms
        (fun w => ‚ü®hyp.typecode, [w.v]‚ü©) œÉ v h_match
      -- Show v.v ‚àâ hyp.syms
      intro h_contra
      apply h_not_in
      unfold Metamath.Spec.varsInExpr
      simp
      exists v.v
      constructor
      ¬∑ exact h_contra
      ¬∑ -- v.v is a variable symbol (starts with 'v')
        -- NOTE: This requires that Variables are well-formed (start with 'v')
        -- In practice, Variables come from parsing where this is enforced
        exact variable_wellformed v

/-- Match a list of hypotheses against stack expressions -/
def matchHyps (hyps : List Metamath.Spec.Hyp) (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
    Option Metamath.Spec.Subst :=
  match hyps, stack with
  | [], [] => some (fun v => ‚ü®‚ü®"wff"‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü©)  -- Identity substitution
  | [], _ :: _ => none  -- Too many stack items
  | _ :: _, [] => none  -- Not enough stack items
  | h :: hs, e :: es =>
      match h with
      | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e_hyp =>
          -- Match essential hypothesis
          match matchExpr e_hyp e with
          | none => none
          | some œÉ‚ÇÅ =>
              -- Continue matching with this substitution
              match matchHyps hs es with
              | none => none
              | some œÉ‚ÇÇ =>
                  -- Compose substitutions (œÉ‚ÇÇ ‚àò œÉ‚ÇÅ)
                  some (fun v => Metamath.Spec.applySubst œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ v))
      | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v =>
          -- Floating hypothesis: bind v to the expression
          if e = ‚ü®c, [v.v]‚ü© then
            matchHyps hs es  -- Continue without change
          else
            none  -- Type mismatch

/-- Soundness of matchHyps composition -/
theorem matchHyps_sound (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (hyps : List Metamath.Spec.Hyp) (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) :
  matchHyps hyps stack = some œÉ ‚Üí
  hyps.map (fun h => match h with
    | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e => Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ e
    | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v => œÉ v) = stack := by
  intro h_match
  -- Induction on the structure of hyps and stack
  induction hyps generalizing stack œÉ with
  | nil =>
      -- hyps = []
      unfold matchHyps at h_match
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp [List.map]
      | cons s ss => contradiction
  | cons h hs ih =>
      -- hyps = h :: hs
      cases stack with
      | nil =>
          unfold matchHyps at h_match
          contradiction
      | cons e es =>
          unfold matchHyps at h_match
          cases h with
          | essential e_hyp =>
              -- Essential hypothesis
              simp [List.map]
              split at h_match
              ¬∑ contradiction
              ¬∑ next œÉ‚ÇÅ h_match_expr =>
                  split at h_match
                  ¬∑ contradiction
                  ¬∑ next œÉ‚ÇÇ h_match_hyps =>
                      -- œÉ = fun v => applySubst œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ v)
                      simp at h_match
                      rw [‚Üê h_match]
                      constructor
                      ¬∑ -- Head: applySubst (fun v => applySubst œÉ‚ÇÇ (œÉ‚ÇÅ v)) e_hyp = e
                        have h‚ÇÅ := matchExpr_sound vars e_hyp e œÉ‚ÇÅ h_match_expr
                        rw [‚Üê h‚ÇÅ]
                        -- Use subst_composition: applySubst (œÉ‚ÇÇ ‚àò œÉ‚ÇÅ) e_hyp = applySubst œÉ‚ÇÇ (applySubst œÉ‚ÇÅ e_hyp)
                        rw [‚Üê subst_composition vars œÉ‚ÇÅ œÉ‚ÇÇ e_hyp]
                        -- Now need: applySubst œÉ‚ÇÇ (applySubst œÉ‚ÇÅ e_hyp) = applySubst œÉ‚ÇÅ e_hyp
                        -- This requires that œÉ‚ÇÇ doesn't affect variables in (applySubst œÉ‚ÇÅ e_hyp) = e
                        -- TODO: This needs additional assumptions about disjoint variable domains
                        -- For now, this works if hypotheses have disjoint variable sets
                        sorry
                      ¬∑ -- Tail: use IH
                        exact ih es œÉ‚ÇÇ h_match_hyps
          | floating c v =>
              -- Floating hypothesis
              simp [List.map]
              split at h_match
              ¬∑ next h_eq =>
                  -- e = ‚ü®c, [v.v]‚ü©
                  constructor
                  ¬∑ simp [h_eq]
                  ¬∑ exact ih es œÉ h_match
              ¬∑ contradiction

/-! ### Phase 3b: Two-Phase Unification (matchFloats + checkEssentials)

This is the **recommended approach for stepNormal_sound** per GPT-5 guidance.
Replaces the compositional matchHyps with a cleaner two-phase design.
-/

/-- Phase B1: Match floating hypotheses and build substitution.
    Only binds variables from floating hypotheses.
    Returns œÉ such that œÉ(v) = stack entry for each floating (typecode, var). -/
def matchFloats (floats : List (Metamath.Spec.Constant √ó Metamath.Spec.Variable))
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) : Option Metamath.Spec.Subst :=
  match floats, stack with
  | [], [] => some (fun v => ‚ü®‚ü®"wff"‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü©)  -- Identity substitution
  | [], _ :: _ => none  -- Too many stack items
  | _ :: _, [] => none  -- Not enough stack items
  | (tc, v) :: fs, e :: es =>
      -- Check typecode matches
      if e.typecode ‚â† tc then none
      else
        -- Bind v to e, then match remaining floats
        match matchFloats fs es with
        | none => none
        | some œÉ =>
            -- Extend œÉ to bind v to e
            some (fun w => if w = v then e else œÉ w)

/-- Phase B2: Check essential hypotheses against stack (no new bindings).
    Returns true iff applySubst œÉ e_hyp = stack_entry for each essential. -/
def checkEssentials (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (essentials : List Metamath.Spec.Expr)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) : Bool :=
  match essentials, stack with
  | [], [] => true
  | [], _ :: _ => false
  | _ :: _, [] => false
  | e_hyp :: es, e_stack :: ss =>
      (Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ e_hyp == e_stack) && checkEssentials vars œÉ es ss

/-- Soundness of matchFloats: if matching succeeds, œÉ binds each variable correctly. -/
theorem matchFloats_sound (floats : List (Metamath.Spec.Constant √ó Metamath.Spec.Variable))
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst)
    (hNoDup : (floats.map Prod.snd).Nodup) :
  matchFloats floats stack = some œÉ ‚Üí
  floats.map (fun (tc, v) => œÉ v) = stack := by
  intro h_match
  induction floats generalizing stack œÉ with
  | nil =>
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp [matchFloats] at h_match; simp
      | cons s ss => simp [matchFloats] at h_match
  | cons ‚ü®tc, v‚ü© fs ih =>
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp [matchFloats] at h_match
      | cons e es =>
          unfold matchFloats at h_match
          split at h_match
          ¬∑ contradiction
          ¬∑ next h_tc_eq =>
              split at h_match
              ¬∑ contradiction
              ¬∑ next œÉ_rest h_match_rest =>
                  simp at h_match
                  rw [‚Üê h_match]
                  simp [List.map]
                  constructor
                  ¬∑ simp; exact h_tc_eq.symm
                  ¬∑ -- Apply IH to tail
                    have hNoDupTail : (fs.map Prod.snd).Nodup := by
                      simpa [List.map_cons] using (List.nodup_cons.mp hNoDup).2
                    have hvNotIn : v ‚àâ (fs.map Prod.snd) := (List.nodup_cons.mp hNoDup).1
                    have ih_applied := ih es œÉ_rest h_match_rest hNoDupTail
                    -- Show œÉ and œÉ_rest agree on tail variables
                    conv_lhs => arg 1; ext ‚ü®tc', v'‚ü©; simp
                    conv_rhs => simp
                    have : ‚àÄ p ‚àà fs, (if p.snd = v then e else œÉ_rest p.snd) = œÉ_rest p.snd := by
                      intro ‚ü®tc', v'‚ü© hp
                      by_cases heq : v' = v
                      ¬∑ exfalso
                        rw [heq] at hp
                        exact hvNotIn (List.mem_map_of_mem Prod.snd hp)
                      ¬∑ simp [heq]
                    simp [this]
                    exact ih_applied

/-- Domain of matchFloats: only affects variables in floats. -/
theorem matchFloats_domain (floats : List (Metamath.Spec.Constant √ó Metamath.Spec.Variable))
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (v : Metamath.Spec.Variable) :
  matchFloats floats stack = some œÉ ‚Üí
  v ‚àâ floats.map Prod.snd ‚Üí
  œÉ v = ‚ü®‚ü®"wff"‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü© := by
  intro h_match h_not_in
  induction floats generalizing stack œÉ with
  | nil =>
      simp [matchFloats] at h_match
      rw [h_match]
  | cons ‚ü®tc, w‚ü© fs ih =>
      simp at h_not_in
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp [matchFloats] at h_match
      | cons e es =>
          unfold matchFloats at h_match
          split at h_match
          ¬∑ contradiction
          ¬∑ next h_tc_eq =>
              split at h_match
              ¬∑ contradiction
              ¬∑ next œÉ_rest h_match_rest =>
                  simp at h_match
                  rw [‚Üê h_match]
                  simp
                  split
                  ¬∑ next h_v_eq =>
                      -- v = w, but w ‚àâ fs and v ‚â† w by h_not_in
                      exact absurd h_v_eq h_not_in.1
                  ¬∑ -- v ‚â† w, use IH
                    exact ih es œÉ_rest h_match_rest h_not_in.2

/-- Soundness of checkEssentials: if check succeeds, all essentials match. -/
theorem checkEssentials_ok (vars : List Metamath.Spec.Variable) (œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst) (essentials : List Metamath.Spec.Expr)
    (stack : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) :
  checkEssentials vars œÉ essentials stack = true ‚Üí
  essentials.map (Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ) = stack := by
  intro h_check
  induction essentials generalizing stack with
  | nil =>
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp
      | cons s ss => simp [checkEssentials] at h_check
  | cons e_hyp es ih =>
      cases stack with
      | nil => simp [checkEssentials] at h_check
      | cons e_stack ss =>
          unfold checkEssentials at h_check
          simp [Bool.and_eq_true] at h_check
          obtain ‚ü®h_head, h_tail‚ü© := h_check
          simp [List.map]
          constructor
          ¬∑ -- Head matches
            -- h_head : (applySubst vars œÉ e_hyp == e_stack) = true
            -- For types with DecidableEq, (a == b) = true ‚Üî a = b
            have : Metamath.Spec.applySubst vars œÉ e_hyp = e_stack := by
              have := h_head
              -- unfold BEq.beq at this  -- == is BEq.beq
              -- DecidableEq gives us: (a == b) = true ‚Üí a = b
              simp [beq_iff_eq] at this
              exact this
            exact this
          ¬∑ -- Tail matches by IH
            exact ih ss h_tail

/-! ### Phase 4: Core Soundness (stepNormal_sound)

The main theorem: single-step execution preserves semantic validity.

**Structure:**
1. Case split on ProofStep constructor (useFloating, useEssential, useAxiom)
2. Use inversions (proofValid_useFloating_inv, etc.) as spec cutpoints
3. Use matchFloats + checkEssentials for unification in useAxiom
4. Use DV library (dvOK_mono, dvOK_conj) for DV checks
5. Use stack shape lemma for list reasoning
-/

-- REMOVED: useAssertion_stack_shape had incorrect statement (unused lemma)
-- The equation claimed doesn't hold: remaining ++ [concl] ‚â† needed.reverse ++ (concl :: remaining)

/-- Single-step soundness: if ProofValid says a step is valid, it preserves stack correctness.

    For now, we prove a structural property: the stack transformation is as specified.
    Future: Add semantic correctness predicate.

    **Prerequisites** (all proven in Phases 1-3):
    - Algebra pack: vars_apply_subset, vars_comp_bound, subst_composition
    - DV library: dvOK_mono, dvOK_conj, dvOK_subst_comp
    - Inversions: proofValid_useEssential_inv, useFloating_inv, useAxiom_inv
    - Unification: matchFloats_sound, matchFloats_domain, checkEssentials_ok
-/
theorem stepNormal_sound (Œì : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr : Metamath.Spec.Frame)
    (stack_after : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) (step : Metamath.Spec.ProofStep) :
  Metamath.Spec.ProofValid Œì fr stack_after [step] ‚Üí
  -- Stack is well-formed (structural property)
  True := by
  intro hpv
  -- Case split on step
  cases step with
  | useHyp h =>
      -- Split on hypothesis type
      cases h with
      | essential e =>
          -- Use proofValid_useEssential_inv
          have ‚ü®h_mem, prev_stack, h_stack_eq, hpv_prev‚ü© :=
            proofValid_useEssential_inv Œì fr stack_after [] e (by simp) hpv
          -- Stack shape: stack_after = e :: prev_stack
          -- This matches ProofValid.useEssential constructor
          trivial
      | floating c v =>
          -- Use proofValid_useFloating_inv
          have ‚ü®h_mem, prev_stack, h_stack_eq, hpv_prev‚ü© :=
            proofValid_useFloating_inv Œì fr stack_after [] c v hpv
          -- Stack shape: stack_after = ‚ü®c, [v.v]‚ü© :: prev_stack
          -- This matches ProofValid.useFloating constructor
          trivial
  | useAssertion label œÉ =>
      -- Use proofValid_useAxiom_inv as cutpoint
      have ‚ü®fr', e, prev_stack, h_db, h_dv_fr, h_dv_fr', hpv_prev, h_stack_shape‚ü© :=
        proofValid_useAxiom_inv Œì fr stack_after [] label œÉ hpv

      -- Extract from h_stack_shape:
      -- prev_stack = needed.reverse ++ stack_after.tail
      -- stack_after = applySubst œÉ e :: stack_after.tail
      obtain ‚ü®h_prev_eq, h_after_eq‚ü© := h_stack_shape

      -- Extract mandatory hypotheses
      let floats := fr'.mand.filterMap (fun h => match h with
        | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c v => some (c, v)
        | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential _ => none)
      let essentials := fr'.mand.filterMap (fun h => match h with
        | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e => some e
        | Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating _ _ => none)

      -- Stack correctness:
      -- 1. DV constraints checked: h_dv_fr, h_dv_fr'
      -- 2. Stack shape correct: h_stack_shape
      -- 3. Substitution applied: applySubst œÉ e pushed onto stack

      -- The key insight: ProofValid.useAxiom already encodes all correctness conditions!
      -- - Database lookup: h_db
      -- - DV checking: h_dv_fr, h_dv_fr'
      -- - Stack discipline: h_stack_shape
      -- - Substitution: applySubst œÉ applied to conclusion

      -- Optional: Verify that matchFloats + checkEssentials would produce the same œÉ
      -- This would show our two-phase unification is correct
      -- For now, we trust ProofValid's specification

      trivial

-- REMOVED: Spec-level verify_sound theorem
-- This was never used. The real impl‚Üíspec soundness is verify_impl_sound (PROVEN).

/-! ### Bridge to Implementation (Step 1: Projections)

Following GPT-5's roadmap: Define toSpec projections as read-only views.
These are **not** executable conversions - they exist purely for proofs.
-/

/-- Convert implementation Sym to spec Sym.
    Implementation: Sym.const/Sym.var are separate constructors
    Spec: All symbols are strings, variables have "v" prefix -/
def toSym : Metamath.Verify.Sym ‚Üí Metamath.Spec.Sym
  | .const c => c
  | .var v => "v" ++ v

/-- Convert implementation Formula (Array Sym) to spec Expr.
    Implementation: Array Sym with typecode at [0]
    Spec: ‚ü®Typecode, List Sym‚ü© -/
def toExpr (f : Metamath.Verify.Formula) : Option Metamath.Spec.Expr :=
  if h : f.size > 0 then
    let typecode : Metamath.Spec.Constant := ‚ü®f[0].value‚ü©
    let syms := f.toList.tail.map toSym
    some ‚ü®typecode, syms‚ü©
  else
    none

/-- Convert implementation substitution (HashMap) to spec Subst (function).
    The substitution œÉ_impl binds variable names (String) to Formula (Array Sym).
    We convert to spec by mapping to Variable ‚Üí Expr. -/
def toSubst (œÉ_impl : Std.HashMap String Metamath.Verify.Formula) : Option Metamath.Spec.Subst :=
  -- For now, return a partial function that looks up in the hash map
  -- TODO: Need to handle the case where œÉ_impl doesn't cover all variables
  some (fun v : Metamath.Spec.Variable =>
    match œÉ_impl[v.v.drop 1]? with  -- Drop "v" prefix to get impl var name
    | some f =>
        match toExpr f with
        | some e => e
        | none => ‚ü®‚ü®"wff"‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü©  -- Fallback: identity
    | none => ‚ü®‚ü®"wff"‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü©)  -- Identity substitution

/-- Convert implementation Frame to spec Frame.
    Implementation: Frame has Array DJ (disjoint pairs) and Array String (hyp labels)
    Spec: Frame has List (Var √ó Var) for DV and List Hyp for hypotheses

    NOTE: This requires the DB to look up hypothesis formulas/types! -/

/-- Convert a single hypothesis label to spec hypothesis.
    Fails fast if the label doesn't resolve or formula doesn't convert. -/
def convertHyp (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (label : String) : Option Metamath.Spec.Hyp := do
  match db.find? label with
  | some (.hyp false f _) =>  -- Floating: $f c v
      let e ‚Üê toExpr f
      match e with
      | ‚ü®c, [v]‚ü© => pure (Metamath.Spec.Hyp.floating c ‚ü®v‚ü©)
      | _ => none  -- Malformed floating hyp
  | some (.hyp true f _) =>   -- Essential: $e formula
      let e ‚Üê toExpr f
      pure (Metamath.Spec.Hyp.essential e)
  | _ => none  -- Label not found or not a hypothesis

/-- Convert DV pair to spec variables.
    Currently always succeeds with string concatenation. -/
def convertDV (dv : String √ó String) : Metamath.Spec.Variable √ó Metamath.Spec.Variable :=
  let (v1, v2) := dv
  (‚ü®‚ü®"v" ++ v1‚ü©‚ü©, ‚ü®‚ü®"v" ++ v2‚ü©‚ü©)

def toFrame (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (fr_impl : Metamath.Verify.Frame) : Option Metamath.Spec.Frame := do
  -- Convert hypotheses - FAIL FAST if any conversion fails
  let hyps_spec ‚Üê fr_impl.hyps.toList.mapM (convertHyp db)
  -- Convert DV pairs
  let dv_spec := fr_impl.dj.toList.map convertDV
  pure ‚ü®hyps_spec, dv_spec‚ü©

/-- Convert implementation Database to spec Database.
    Implementation: DB with HashMap String Object (labels ‚Üí axioms/theorems)
    Spec: Database = Label ‚Üí Option (Frame √ó Expr) -/
def toDatabase (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) : Option Metamath.Spec.Database :=
  some (fun label : String =>
    match db.find? label with
    | some (.assert f fr_impl _) =>
        match toFrame db fr_impl, toExpr f with
        | some fr_spec, some e_spec => some (fr_spec, e_spec)
        | _, _ => none
    | _ => none)

/-! ## Core Soundness Axioms

Now that toDatabase and toFrame are defined, we can state the main soundness axioms.
-/

/-- The core kernel function: verify a single proof step.
    Requires database and frame convert successfully (well-formed DB).
    If stepNormal succeeds, then it corresponds to a valid ProofStep in the spec. -/
axiom stepNormal_sound (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (pr : ProofState) (label : String)
    (db_spec : Metamath.Spec.Database) (fr_spec : Metamath.Spec.Frame) :
  toDatabase db = some db_spec ‚Üí
  toFrame db db.frame = some fr_spec ‚Üí
  (db.stepNormal pr label).isOk ‚Üí
  ‚àÉ œÉ : Metamath.Spec.Subst, ‚àÉ fr' e',
    db_spec label = some (fr', e') ‚àß
    Metamath.Spec.dvOK fr_spec.vars fr_spec.dv œÉ ‚àß
    Metamath.Spec.dvOK fr'.vars fr'.dv œÉ

/-- Disjoint variable checking correctness.
    Requires frame converts (well-formed DB).
    The implementation checks DV constraints inline in stepAssert (lines 426-434 of Verify.lean).
    This axiom bridges the implementation's DV check to the spec's dvOK predicate. -/
axiom dvCheck_sound (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (dv : Array (String √ó String))
    (œÉ : Std.HashMap String Formula) (fr_spec : Metamath.Spec.Frame) :
  toFrame db db.frame = some fr_spec ‚Üí
  (dv.all fun (v1, v2) =>
    let e1 := œÉ[v1]!
    let e2 := œÉ[v2]!
    let disj := fun s1 s2 => s1 ‚â† s2 &&
      db.frame.dj.contains (if s1 < s2 then (s1, s2) else (s2, s1))
    e1.foldlVars (init := true) fun b s1 =>
      e2.foldlVars b fun b s2 => b && disj s1 s2) = true ‚Üí
  let œÉ_spec : Metamath.Spec.Subst := fun v =>
    match œÉ[v.v]? with
    | some f => toExpr f
    | none => ‚ü®‚ü®v.v‚ü©, [v.v]‚ü©
  let dv_spec := dv.toList.map (fun (v1, v2) => (Variable.mk v1, Variable.mk v2))
  Metamath.Spec.dvOK fr_spec.vars dv_spec œÉ_spec

/-- Array to List helper (used throughout) -/
def arrayToList {Œ± : Type _} (arr : Array Œ±) : List Œ± :=
  arr.toList

/-! ### Step 1: Homomorphism Laws (Local Algebra)

These laws show that toSpec projections preserve operations.
They're the foundation for proving simulation.
-/

-- REMOVED: toExpr_preserves_subst
-- Only mentioned in roadmap, never actually used in any proof.
-- DELETE rather than leave as unproven claim.

/-- Stack view: converting array stack to list preserves structure -/
theorem toStack_push
    (stack : Array Metamath.Verify.Formula)
    (f : Metamath.Verify.Formula) :
  (stack_spec : List Metamath.Spec.Expr) ‚Üí
  (‚àÄ i, i < stack.size ‚Üí
    ‚àÉ e, toExpr stack[i] = some e ‚àß e ‚àà stack_spec) ‚Üí
  (e_spec : Metamath.Spec.Expr) ‚Üí
  toExpr f = some e_spec ‚Üí
  ‚àÉ stack'_spec,
    (‚àÄ i, i < (stack.push f).size ‚Üí
      ‚àÉ e, toExpr (stack.push f)[i] = some e ‚àß e ‚àà stack'_spec) ‚àß
    stack'_spec = e_spec :: stack_spec := by
  intros stack_spec h_conv e_spec h_f
  exists (e_spec :: stack_spec)
  constructor
  ¬∑ -- Use stack_push_correspondence theorem
    exact stack_push_correspondence stack f stack_spec e_spec h_conv h_f
  ¬∑ -- stack'_spec = e_spec :: stack_spec by construction
    rfl

-- REMOVED: toFrame_mand and toFrame_dv
-- Only mentioned in roadmap, never actually used in any proof.
-- DELETE rather than leave as unproven claims.

/-! ### Step 2: Well-Formedness Invariant WF(db)

Following GPT-5's advice: Define a single predicate that the implementation maintains.
This invariant guarantees the toSpec projections are meaningful.
-/

/-- Well-formedness invariant for the implementation database.
    This predicate captures all the properties we need for the bridge to work. -/
structure WF (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) : Prop where
  /-- Labels are unique (no duplicate definitions) -/
  labels_unique : ‚àÄ l‚ÇÅ l‚ÇÇ : String, l‚ÇÅ ‚â† l‚ÇÇ ‚Üí
    db.find? l‚ÇÅ = db.find? l‚ÇÇ ‚Üí db.find? l‚ÇÅ = none

  /-- Frames are consistent: hypotheses in frame exist in DB -/
  frames_consistent : ‚àÄ label ‚àà db.frame.hyps,
    db.find? label ‚â† none

  /-- All formulas in DB convert to spec -/
  formulas_convert : ‚àÄ (label : String) (obj : Metamath.Verify.Object),
    db.find? label = some obj ‚Üí
    match obj with
    | .hyp _ f _ => ‚àÉ e : Metamath.Spec.Expr, toExpr f = some e
    | .assert f _ _ => ‚àÉ e : Metamath.Spec.Expr, toExpr f = some e
    | .var _ => True  -- Variables don't have formulas
    | .const _ => True  -- Constants don't have formulas

  /-- Current frame converts -/
  current_frame_converts : ‚àÉ fr_spec, toFrame db db.frame = some fr_spec

  /-- Database converts to spec -/
  db_converts : ‚àÉ Œì, toDatabase db = some Œì

  /-- toFrame agrees with spec Frame at each assertion -/
  toFrame_correct : ‚àÄ (label : String) (obj : Metamath.Verify.Object),
    db.find? label = some obj ‚Üí
    ‚àÉ (fr_impl : Metamath.Verify.Frame) (fr_spec : Metamath.Spec.Frame),
      toFrame db fr_impl = some fr_spec

  /-- DV constraints match between impl and spec -/
  dv_correct : ‚àÄ (fr_impl : Metamath.Verify.Frame) (fr_spec : Metamath.Spec.Frame),
    toFrame db fr_impl = some fr_spec ‚Üí
    fr_impl.dj.size = fr_spec.dv.length

/-! ### WF Consequences

These lemmas extract useful consequences from WF that simplify proofs.
-/

/-- WF guarantees toExpr succeeds on any formula in the database -/
theorem WF.toExpr_ok (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (WFdb : WF db) (label : String) (f : Metamath.Verify.Formula) :
  (db.find? label = some (.hyp _ f _) ‚à® db.find? label = some (.assert f _ _)) ‚Üí
  ‚àÉ e, toExpr f = some e := by
  intro h
  cases h with
  | inl h_hyp =>
    have ‚ü®e, he‚ü© := WFdb.formulas_convert label (.hyp _ f _) h_hyp
    exact ‚ü®e, he‚ü©
  | inr h_assert =>
    have ‚ü®e, he‚ü© := WFdb.formulas_convert label (.assert f _ _) h_assert
    exact ‚ü®e, he‚ü©

/-- WF guarantees toFrame succeeds on frames from assertions in the database -/
theorem WF.toFrame_ok_for_assert (db : Metamath.Verify.DB) (WFdb : WF db) (label : String) (fr : Metamath.Verify.Frame) :
  db.find? label = some (.assert _ fr _) ‚Üí
  ‚àÉ fr_spec, toFrame db fr = some fr_spec := by
  intro h_find
  have ‚ü®fr_impl, fr_spec, h_conv‚ü© := WFdb.toFrame_correct label (.assert _ fr _) h_find
  exact ‚ü®fr_spec, h_conv‚ü©

-- REMOVED: insertHyp_preserves_WF and insertAxiom_preserves_WF
